[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the curl library during [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **stack-buffer-overflow** vulnerability with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow. The overflow occurs when [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting beyond the bounds of a stack-allocated array.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during the following sequence:[0m                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Buffer boundaries**: [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m480[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m bytes allocated[0m                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m498[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m499[0m[39m:    else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m500[0m[39m:      result = [0m[1;35mCurl_client_write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, CLIENTWRITE_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER,[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m501[0m[39m:                                 body_msg, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbody_msg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m502[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m410[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m412[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m413[0m[39m: * [0m[1;35mfile_do[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is the protocol-specific function for the do-phase, separated[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m414[0m[39m: * from the connect-phase above. Other protocols merely setup the transfer in[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m415[0m[39m: * the do-phase, to have it done in the main transfer loop but since some[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m416[0m[39m: * platforms we support do not allow [0m[1;35mselect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39ming etc on file handles [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m417[0m[39m: * opposed to sockets[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m we instead perform the whole do-operation in this[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m418[0m[39m: * function.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m419[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m420[0m[39m:static CURLcode [0m[1;35mfile_do[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstruct Curl_easy *data, bool *done[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m421[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m422[0m[39m:  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* This implementation ignores the hostname in conformance with[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m423[0m[39m:     RFC [0m[1;36m1738[0m[39m. Only local files [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreachable via the standard file system[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m424[0m[39m:     are supported. This means that files on remotely mounted directories[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m425[0m[39m:     [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia NFS, Samba, NT sharing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can be accessed through a [0m[4;94mfile://[0m[39m URL[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m426[0m[39m:  *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m427[0m[39m:  CURLcode result = CURLE_OK;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m428[0m[39m:  struct_stat statbuf; [0m[35m/[0m[39m* struct_stat instead of struct stat just to allow the[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m429[0m[39m:                          Windows version to have a different struct without[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m430[0m[39m:                          having to redefine the simple word [0m[32m'stat'[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlib/file.[0m[1;92mc:520[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m560[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m520[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m521[0m[39m:      return result;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m522[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* set the file size to make it available post transfer *[0m[35m/[0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I can identify the root [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAt `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mfile.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m495[0m[39m`, there is a critical bug where `msnprintf` is called [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith incorrect parameters:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mmsnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mno_body[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[32m"%s [0m[32m([0m[32m%ld bytes[0m[32m)[0m[32m \r\n"[0m[39m, no_body, expected_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issues are:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Buffer size parameter mismatch**: Uses `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mno_body[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m~[0m[1;36m145[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m80[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Wrong format specifier**: Uses `%ld` instead of `%[0m[32m" FMT_OFF_T "[0m[39m` for the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`curl_off_t` type[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Inherent design flaw**: The `no_body` static string alone is ~[0m[1;36m145[0m[39m characters, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich already exceeds the [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-byte `header` buffer even before adding the formatted [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte count[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `mprintf` implementation trusts the `maxlength` parameter [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1073[0m[39m in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmprintf.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and will write up to that many bytes, regardless of the actual buffer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize. When `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mno_body[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m~[0m[1;36m145[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is passed but the buffer is only [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes, it writes beyond the buffer boundary, causing a stack buffer overflow.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Insights from Code Analysis[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Established patterns in the codebase**: [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Static strings like `accept_ranges` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m482[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m485[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `body_msg` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m500[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m501[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are written directly using `Curl_client_write` without formatting[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Dynamic headers like Content-Length [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m475[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and Last-Modified [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m507[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly use `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with `msnprintf`[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Test compatibility**: The test case at `tests/libtest/lib3208.[0m[1;92mc:48[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m49[0m[39m` only [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidates that the header starts with [0m[32m"File-body"[0m[39m, not the complete content. This [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmeans we can modify the header format without breaking tests.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Redundancy**: The byte count in the `no_body` message is redundant because the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mContent-Length header [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m474[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m480[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already provides the file size information.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix should be applied to `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mfile.c[0m[39m` at lines [0m[1;36m493[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m502[0m[39m:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Replace the buggy formatting code[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemove the `msnprintf` call at lines [0m[1;36m494[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m496[0m[39m that attempts to format the `no_body` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring with byte count information into the [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-byte `header` buffer.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Write the static string directly[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFollow the established pattern used for `body_msg` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m500[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m501[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`accept_ranges` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m482[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m485[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m by writing the `no_body` static string directly [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout formatting:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->req.no_body[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  result = [0m[1;35mCurl_client_write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, CLIENTWRITE_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER,[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                             no_body, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mno_body[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis approach:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Eliminates the buffer overflow by removing the intermediate `header` buffer usage[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Writes the complete `no_body` message without truncation[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Matches the established pattern for static header strings in the codebase[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains protocol compatibility [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe File-body header is still sent[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Passes existing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich only check for [0m[32m"File-body"[0m[39m prefix[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removes the redundant byte count [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready provided by Content-Length header[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Verification[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix preserves all existing functionality:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Headers are written in the same order: Content-Length → Accept-ranges → File-body[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m→ Last-Modified[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The File-body header is still sent when `data->req.no_body` is true[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The message still indicates the body is suppressed with usage instructions[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to the `header` buffer usage for Content-Length and Last-Modified [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheaders[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to test codes or harness codes[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal code change**: Only modifies the buggy section [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m493[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m502[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreducing risk of introducing new issues[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows established patterns**: Uses the same approach as `body_msg` and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`accept_ranges` headers in the same function[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Eliminates all three bugs simultaneously**:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Buffer overflow: No longer uses the `header` buffer for this message[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Format specifier mismatch: No longer uses `%ld` for `curl_off_t`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Design flaw: Can now write the complete message without size constraints[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Maintains backward compatibility**: The File-body header is still sent with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same prefix, satisfying test requirements[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No information loss that matters**: The byte count is redundant since [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mContent-Length header already provides file size[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All header writing logic remains unchanged except for the buggy `no_body` case[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-byte `header` buffer continues to be used correctly for Content-Length and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLast-Modified headers[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The control flow for `fstated` block remains identical[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The early return at line [0m[1;36m525[0m[39m when `data->req.no_body` is true remains unchanged[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No impact on file reading/transfer logic below line [0m[1;36m527[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effect**: The File-body header will no longer include the byte [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcount like [0m[32m"File-body: suppressed... [0m[32m([0m[32m12345 bytes[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: This is acceptable because:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The Content-Length header already provides this information[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The existing test only validates the [0m[32m"File-body"[0m[39m prefix[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The message still serves its purpose of informing users the body is suppressed[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The byte count was incorrectly formatted anyway [0m[1;39m([0m[39musing `%ld` for `curl_off_t`[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe exact same pattern is used at lines [0m[1;36m500[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m501[0m[39m for the `body_msg`:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresult = [0m[1;35mCurl_client_write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, CLIENTWRITE_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER,[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           body_msg, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbody_msg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAnd at lines [0m[1;36m482[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m485[0m[39m for `accept_ranges`:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresult = [0m[1;35mCurl_client_write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, CLIENTWRITE_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER,[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           accept_ranges, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39maccept_ranges[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis proves the approach is well-established and safe in the curl codebase.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>lib/file.[0m[1;92mc:493[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m502[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
